<date>1533689420857<//date><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
The Disney Store is amazing because it deals in memories and nostalgia all while being cool at the same time.
There are items for children of all ages, including us adult children.
There are toys, clothing, housewares, collectibles and more that relate to the huge amount of storylines Disney has brought to us from back in the 1940's to the present. These storylines include Winnie the Pooh, all of the Disney Princesses, the Star Wars galaxy and even the Marvel Universe.
The products related to the stories and movies touch us in a way that seems to be more meaningful than the standard make a movie release the swag concept.
Disney has gone beyond that idea touching our feelings in a way nobody else has equaled.
I am definitely going back!< /Review>

He started to describe his symptoms. At the time, I didn't know what was really going on but I knew he showing some sign of a stroke. So I took him to Dameron and we didn't wait too long a the E.R. My advise is to always go with your gut feeling and never take people word because even if they are doctor, they might not be the best one. <review>Funky little place off of Divis where all sorts of people hang out - the crowd had some older couples, college kids, etc. It gets really crowded on a weekend night as the evening goes on and I believe there's a cover after 9 PM. Honestly, the cover didn't seem worth it so I was glad I went in before they began charging. If you want a quieter place to talk with your friends and not get consistently bumped into, this is not the place. < review>
Pretty crowded on a Thursday night, and found that people were a bit more hesitant to dance than the music invited (maybe it was just the night/time I was there).

I like the space a lot, and a pretty large bar in the back. The music was super fun dancing music, too.

The location is awesome, right on the Wiggle (if you're by bike) or Divis (if you're in the city).

I would definitely check it out again, it's always pretty busy and have seen big linds on the weekend (rightfully so -  michael jackson night!)</review>
